## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillator dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves finding the acceleration (dv/dt) of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator as a function of position x, velocity v, and time t. The acceleration in such systems typically arises from restoring forces (functions of x) and damping forces (functions of v), possibly with nonlinear terms like cubic stiffness (Duffing) or nonlinear damping (van der Pol).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Simple harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (linear restoring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring + linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring + damping)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (1 - c2 * x**2) * v (nonlinear damping)
- Quintic nonlinear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order restoring force)
- Quadratic nonlinear restoring: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 (asymmetric nonlinear restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping with cubic velocity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (nonlinear velocity damping)
- Forced oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (periodic external driving)
- Position-velocity coupling: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x * v (multiplicative coupling term)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (Rayleigh-type nonlinear damping)
- General cubic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * x**3 + c3 * v (full cubic polynomial restoring + damping)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * cos(c1 * t) (time-varying stiffness)
- Softening/hardening spring with damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * x**2 * v (Duffing + nonlinear damping)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear restoring force → term proportional to -x (simple harmonic behavior, oscillatory solutions)
- Cubic position term (x**3) → Duffing-type hardening/softening nonlinearity causing amplitude-dependent frequency
- Velocity-dependent terms with x**2 prefactor → van der Pol type self-sustained oscillation (limit cycles)
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x**3, x**5) → symmetric potential wells preserving oscillation symmetry
- Even-power restoring forces (x**2) → asymmetric potential breaking oscillation symmetry
- Sinusoidal time dependence sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) → external periodic forcing causing resonance phenomena
- Product terms x*v → energy-dependent damping or conservative nonlinear coupling
- Negative linear damping + positive cubic velocity damping → self-excited oscillation with amplitude saturation (Rayleigh/van der Pol)
- Absence of explicit time dependence → autonomous system, phase-plane analysis applicable

`-1.1056075693807*x - 1.1056075693807*x = -2.2112151387614*x`

So GT = `-2.2112151387614*x - 0.0610726519698*x*Abs(v)**(1/3) - 0.0230405406738805*v**3 + 0.350781823399691*sin(t)`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `x` (linear)
2. `x * |v|^(1/3)` (nonlinear cross-term)
3. `v^3` (cubic in v)
4. `sin(t)`

This is a very specific set of basis functions. The key distinguishing term is `x * |v|^(1/3)`, which involves a fractional power of the absolute value of v.

Let me now check each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `c0*x + c1*v + c2*sin(t) + c3*sin(c4*(c5*x + c6*v))`
Has `v` (linear) and `sin(linear combo)` — no `v^3` or `x*|v|^(1/3)`. Cannot match.
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `c0*x + c1*sin(t) + c2*v*sin(c3*t + c4) + c5*v**2*x + c6*v**3`
Has `v*sin(c3*t+c4)` and `v^2*x` instead of `x*|v|^(1/3)`. Setting c2=0 removes the v*sin term, but then we'd need `x*|v|^(1/3)` from `v^2*x`, which is impossible.
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `c0*x + c1*sin(t) + c2*v*cos(c3*t) + c4*v**2*x + c5*x**3 + c6*v**3`
Missing `x*|v|^(1/3)`. Has `v*cos(c3*t)`, `v^2*x`, `x^3` — none can produce `x*|v|^(1/3)`.
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2 + t) + c3*v*cos(c4*t) + c5*v**2*x + c6*v + c7*v**3`
Missing `x*|v|^(1/3)`. No term can produce it.
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** `c0*x + c1*sin(c2 + t) + c3*v*cos(c4*t) + c5*v**2*x + c6*v**3`
Same issue — missing `x*|v|^(1/3)`.
Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 6:** `c0*x + c1*sin(t) + c2*v*cos(c3*t) + c4*v**3 + c5*v**2*x`
Missing `x*|v|^(1/3)`.
Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 7:** `c0*x + c1*sin(t) + c2*v**2*x + c3*x**3 + c4*v**3`
Missing `x*|v|^(1/3)`.
Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 8:** `c0*x + c1*sin(t) + c2*sin(c3*v) + c4*v + c5*v**2*x`
`sin(c3*v)` is not `|v|^(1/3)*x`. Missing required terms.
Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 9:** `c0*x + c1*sin(t) + c2*v**3 + c3*v**2*x`
Missing `x*|v|^(1/3)`.
Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 10-55:** All candidates use polynomial terms in v and x (like `v*cos(t)`, `v^2*x`, `x^3`, `v*x^2`, `log(v+1)`, `x^c`, etc.) but none contain `|v|^(1/3)*x` or any equivalent fractional power of |v| multiplied by x.

Let me check **Candidate 31:** `c0*x + c1*sin(t) + c2*x**c3 + c4*v**3` — has `x^c3` but needs `x*|v|^(1/3)`, not a power of x alone.
Candidate 31 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 29:** `c0*x + c1*sin(t) + c2*v**3 + c3*x**c4 + c5*v*x**2` — `x^c4` doesn't help.
Candidate 29 verdict: [NO MATCH]

For all remaining candidates (10-30, 32-55), none contain `x*|v|^(1/3)` or any equivalent term. They all use integer powers or trigonometric/logarithmic functions that cannot produce this fractional power cross-term.

Candidates 10-28, 30, 32-55 verdict: [NO MATCH]
